Table: users
  - id (bigint(20) unsigned) [PRI]
  - name (varchar(255)) 
  - username (varchar(255)) [UNI]
  - email (varchar(255)) [UNI]
  - nik (varchar(20)) 
  - email_verified_at (timestamp) 
  - password (varchar(255)) 
  - remember_token (varchar(100)) 
  - created_at (timestamp) 
  - updated_at (timestamp) 

Table: utd_cekal_darah
  - no_donor (varchar(15)) [PRI]
  - tanggal (date) 
  - dinas (enum('Pagi','Siang','Sore','Malam')) 
  - petugas_pemusnahan (varchar(20)) [MUL]
  - keterangan (varchar(100)) 
  Foreign Keys:
    -> no_donor references utd_donor(no_donor)
    -> petugas_pemusnahan references petugas(nip)

Table: utd_detail_pemisahan_komponen
  - no_donor (varchar(15)) [MUL]
  - no_kantong (varchar(20)) [PRI]
  - kode_komponen (varchar(5)) 
  - tanggal_kadaluarsa (date) 
  Foreign Keys:
    -> no_donor references utd_pemisahan_komponen(no_donor)

Table: utd_donor
  - no_donor (varchar(15)) [PRI]
  - no_pendonor (varchar(15)) [MUL]
  - tanggal (date) 
  - dinas (enum('Pagi','Siang','Sore','Malam')) 
  - tensi (varchar(7))
